default_air_unit_production = {
	enable = { always = yes }
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes
	ai_strategy = {
		type = unit_ratio
		id = fighter
		value = 96
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = unit_ratio
		id = cas
		value = 24
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = unit_ratio
		id = tactical_bomber
		value = 24
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = unit_ratio
		id = strategic_bomber
		value = 24
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = unit_ratio
		id = naval_bomber
		value = 24
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = equipment_production_factor
		id = heavy_fighter
		value = -48
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = unit_ratio
		id = heavy_fighter
		value = 24
	}
}

bba_air_prod_1 = {
	enable = {
		date < 1730.1.1
	}
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes

	ai_strategy = {
		type = unit_ratio
		id = fighter
		value = 300
	}

	ai_strategy = {
		type = equipment_production_factor
		id = fighter
		value = 200
	}

	ai_strategy = {
		type = equipment_production_min_factories
		id = fighter
		value = 6
	}

		id = cas
		value = -25 #because doctrine this = 15

	}

	}

		value = -20
	}

		value = 3
	}

	}

		value = -100

	ai_strategy = {

aNCFO_air_production = {
	allowed = { is_major = yes }
	enable = { always = yes }
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes
	
	ai_strategy = { type = air_factory_balance value = 80 }
}

aNCFO_focus_on_fighters = {
	allowed = { is_major = yes }
	enable = { 
		has_tech = basic_small_airframe
		has_deployed_air_force_size = { size < 3000 type = fighter }
	}
	abort = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				has_tech = basic_small_airframe
				has_deployed_air_force_size = { size < 3500 type = fighter }
			}
		}
	}

	ai_strategy = { type = unit_ratio id = fighter value = 100 }
}

aNCFO_sideline_on_fighters_deployed = {
	allowed = { is_major = yes }
	enable = { 
		has_tech = basic_small_airframe
		has_deployed_air_force_size = { size > 12000 type = fighter }
	}
	abort = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				has_tech = basic_small_airframe
				has_deployed_air_force_size = { size > 15000 type = fighter }
			}
		}
	}

	ai_strategy = { type = unit_ratio id = fighter value = -110 }

	ai_strategy = { type = equipment_production_factor id = fighter value = -110 }

	ai_strategy = { type = unit_ratio id = cas value = 20 }

	ai_strategy = { type = equipment_production_factor id = cas value = 20 }

	ai_strategy = { type = unit_ratio id = tactical_bomber value = 40 }

	ai_strategy = { type = equipment_production_factor id = tactical_bomber value = 40 }

	ai_strategy = { type = unit_ratio id = strategic_bomber value = 30 }

	ai_strategy = { type = equipment_production_factor id = strategic_bomber value = 30 }
}

aNCFO_sideline_on_fighters_stockpile = {
	allowed = { is_major = yes }
	enable = {  OR = {
		has_deployed_air_force_size = { size > 18000 type = fighter }
		has_equipment = { small_plane_airframe > 21000 }
	} }
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes

	ai_strategy = { type = unit_ratio id = fighter value = -110 }

	ai_strategy = { type = equipment_production_factor id = fighter value = -110 }

	ai_strategy = { type = unit_ratio id = cas value = 20 }

	ai_strategy = { type = equipment_production_factor id = cas value = 20 }

	ai_strategy = { type = unit_ratio id = tactical_bomber value = 40 }

	ai_strategy = { type = equipment_production_factor id = tactical_bomber value = 40 }

	ai_strategy = { type = unit_ratio id = strategic_bomber value = 30 }

	ai_strategy = { type = equipment_production_factor id = strategic_bomber value = 30 }
}

aNCFO_naval_bombers = {
	allowed = { is_major = yes }
	enable = { 
		has_tech = basic_small_airframe
		has_deployed_air_force_size = { size < 400 type = naval_bomber }
		num_of_military_factories > 50
	}
	abort = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				has_tech = basic_small_airframe
				has_deployed_air_force_size = { size < 800 type = naval_bomber }
				num_of_military_factories > 50
			}
		}	
	}

	ai_strategy = { type = equipment_production_min_factories id = naval_bomber value = 5 }
}

aNCFO_build_patrol_bombers = {
	enable = {
		has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
		has_navy_size = { size > 25 }
	}
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes

	ai_strategy = {
		type = unit_ratio
		id = maritime_patrol_plane
		value = 3
	}
}

aNCFO_build_more_patrol_bombers = {
	enable = {
		has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
		has_navy_size = { size > 100 }
		is_major = yes
	}
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes

	ai_strategy = {
		type = unit_ratio
		id = maritime_patrol_plane
		value = 10
	}

	ai_strategy = {
		type = equipment_production_factor
		id = maritime_patrol_plane
		value = 15
	}
}

default_spyplanes_production = {
	enable = {
		is_major = yes
		OR = {
			OR = {
				has_tech = scout_plane1
				has_tech = photo_reconnaisance
			}
			#has_equipment = {
			#	scout_plane_equipment > 50
			#}
			has_deployed_air_force_size = {
				size > 50
				type = scout_plane
			}
		}
	}

	abort_when_not_enabled = yes

	ai_strategy = {
		type = unit_ratio
		id = scout_plane
		value = -99
	}

	ai_strategy = {
		type = equipment_production_factor
		id = scout_plane
		value = -99
	}

	ai_strategy = {
		type = equipment_production_min_factories
		id = scout_plane
		value = 1
	}
}

minors_dont_spy = {
	enable = {
		OR = {
			has_tech = scout_plane1
			has_tech = photo_reconnaisance
		}
		is_major = no
	}

	abort_when_not_enabled = yes

	ai_strategy = {
		type = unit_ratio
		id = scout_plane
		value = -10
	}
}
# Location Radar Station
	location_airbase_1 = {
		enable = { date > 1938.1.1
			1 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				any_neighbor_state = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = no
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_war_with_major = yes
				AND = {
					is_major = yes
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
		}
		abort_when_not_enabled = yes
		ai_strategy = {
			type = build_building
			id = air_base
			target = 1
			value = 100
		}
